SELECT player_name
FROM (
  SELECT T1.player_name, T1.height, AVG(T2.finishing) AS avg_finishing
  FROM Player AS T1
  INNER JOIN Player_Attributes AS T2
    ON T1.player_api_id = T2.player_api_id
  GROUP BY T1.player_api_id, T1.player_name, T1.height
) AS sub
WHERE sub.height = (SELECT MAX(height) FROM Player)
   OR sub.height = (SELECT MIN(height) FROM Player)
ORDER BY avg_finishing DESC, player_name ASC
LIMIT 1;

```python
db.execute("""
WITH ariel AS (
  SELECT pa.overall_rating AS rating
  FROM Player p
  JOIN Player_Attributes pa
    ON p.player_api_id = pa.player_api_id
  WHERE p.player_name = 'Ariel Borysiuk'
  ORDER BY pa.date DESC
  LIMIT 1
),
paulin AS (
  SELECT pa.overall_rating AS rating
  FROM Player p
  JOIN Player_Attributes pa
    ON p.player_api_id = pa.player_api_id
  WHERE p.player_name = 'Paulin Puel'
  ORDER BY pa.date DESC
  LIMIT 1
)
SELECT 100.0 * (ariel.rating - paulin.rating) / paulin.rating AS percentage_higher
FROM ariel, paulin;
```

SELECT e.Symptoms, e.Diagnosis
FROM Examination AS e
INNER JOIN Patient AS p ON e.ID = p.ID
WHERE e.Symptoms IS NOT NULL
  AND p.Birthday = (
    SELECT MAX(p2.Birthday)
    FROM Patient AS p2
    INNER JOIN Examination AS e2 ON p2.ID = e2.ID
    WHERE e2.Symptoms IS NOT NULL
  )
ORDER BY e."Examination Date" DESC
LIMIT 1

SELECT e.expense_description, e.approved
FROM expense AS e
JOIN budget AS b ON e.link_to_budget = b.budget_id
JOIN event AS ev ON b.link_to_event = ev.event_id
WHERE ev.event_name = 'October Meeting'
  AND date(ev.event_date) = '2019-10-08'
ORDER BY e.expense_description;

FINAL("WITH annuals AS (
  SELECT c.Segment, ym.CustomerID, SUM(ym.Consumption) AS total_consumption
  FROM yearmonth AS ym
  JOIN customers AS c
    ON ym.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
  WHERE c.Currency = 'CZK'
    AND substr(ym.Date, 1, 4) = '2013'
    AND c.Segment IN ('SME', 'LAM', 'KAM')
  GROUP BY c.Segment, ym.CustomerID
),
minvals AS (
  SELECT Segment, MIN(total_consumption) AS min_consumption
  FROM annuals
  GROUP BY Segment
),
segment_avg AS (
  SELECT a.Segment,
         SUM(a.total_consumption) * 1.0 / COUNT(*) AS annual_average
  FROM annuals AS a
  JOIN minvals AS m
    ON a.Segment = m.Segment
   AND a.total_consumption = m.min_consumption
  GROUP BY a.Segment
)
SELECT
  MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'SME' THEN annual_average END) - MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'LAM' THEN annual_average END) AS SME_LAM_difference,
  MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'LAM' THEN annual_average END) - MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'KAM' THEN annual_average END) AS LAM_KAM_difference,
  MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'KAM' THEN annual_average END) - MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'SME' THEN annual_average END) AS KAM_SME_difference
FROM segment_avg;")

```python
db.execute("""
WITH annuals AS (
  SELECT
    c.Segment,
    ym.CustomerID,
    SUM(ym.Consumption) AS annual_consumption
  FROM yearmonth AS ym
  JOIN customers AS c
    ON ym.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
  WHERE c.Currency = 'CZK'
    AND ym.Date BETWEEN '201301' AND '201312'
    AND c.Segment IN ('SME', 'LAM', 'KAM')
  GROUP BY c.Segment, ym.CustomerID
),
min_by_segment AS (
  SELECT Segment, MIN(annual_consumption) AS min_consumption
  FROM annuals
  GROUP BY Segment
),
segment_avg AS (
  SELECT
    a.Segment,
    AVG(a.annual_consumption) AS annual_average
  FROM annuals AS a
  JOIN min_by_segment AS m
    ON a.Segment = m.Segment
   AND a.annual_consumption = m.min_consumption
  GROUP BY a.Segment
)
SELECT
  MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'SME' THEN annual_average END) - MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'LAM' THEN annual_average END) AS SME_LAM_difference,
  MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'LAM' THEN annual_average END) - MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'KAM' THEN annual_average END) AS LAM_KAM_difference,
  MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'KAM' THEN annual_average END) - MAX(CASE WHEN Segment = 'SME' THEN annual_average END) AS KAM_SME_difference
FROM segment_avg;
""")
```

FINAL("WITH annual_consumption AS (
  SELECT
    c.Segment,
    ym.CustomerID,
    SUM(ym.Consumption) AS annual_consumption
  FROM yearmonth AS ym
  JOIN customers AS c
    ON ym.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
  WHERE c.Currency = 'CZK'
    AND substr(ym.Date, 1, 4) = '2013'
    AND c.Segment IN ('SME', 'LAM', 'KAM')
  GROUP BY c.Segment, ym.CustomerID
),
lowest_consumption AS (
  SELECT
    Segment,
    MIN(annual_consumption) AS min_annual_consumption
  FROM annual_consumption
  GROUP BY Segment
),
segment_avg AS (
  SELECT
    ac.Segment,
    AVG(ac.annual_consumption) AS annual_avg
  FROM annual_consumption AS ac
  JOIN lowest_consumption AS lc
    ON ac.Segment = lc.Segment
   AND ac.annual_consumption = lc.min_annual_consumption
  GROUP BY ac.Segment
)
SELECT
  (SELECT annual_avg FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'SME') - (SELECT annual_avg FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'LAM') AS SME_LAM_difference,
  (SELECT annual_avg FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'LAM') - (SELECT annual_avg FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'KAM') AS LAM_KAM_difference,

🤖 model turn:

```python
sql = """
WITH segment_year AS (
  SELECT
    c.Segment AS segment,
    CAST(substr(y.Date, 1, 4) AS INTEGER) AS yr,
    SUM(y.Consumption) AS consumption
  FROM yearmonth y
  JOIN customers c ON y.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
  WHERE c.Currency = 'EUR'
    AND c.Segment IN ('SME', 'LAM', 'KAM')
    AND substr(y.Date, 1, 4) IN ('2012', '2013')
  GROUP BY c.Segment, CAST(substr(y.Date, 1, 4) AS INTEGER)
),
pivot AS (
  SELECT
    segment,
    SUM(CASE WHEN yr = 2012 THEN consumption ELSE 0 END) AS consumption_2012,
    SUM(CASE WHEN yr = 2013 THEN consumption ELSE 0 END) AS consumption_2013
  FROM segment_year
  GROUP BY segment
),
calc AS (
  SELECT
    segment,
    (consumption_2013 - consumption_2012) * 100.0 / NULLIF(consumption_2013, 0) AS pct_increase
  FROM pivot
),
ranked AS (
  SELECT
    segment,
    pct_increase,
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY pct_increase DESC) AS rn_desc,
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY pct_increase ASC) AS rn_asc
  FROM calc
)
SELECT
  (SELECT segment FROM ranked WHERE rn_desc = 1) AS biggest_segment,
  (SELECT pct_increase FROM ranked WHERE rn_desc = 1) AS biggest_percentage_increase,
  (SELECT segment FROM ranked WHERE rn_asc = 1) AS lowest_segment,
  (SELECT pct_increase FROM ranked WHERE rn_asc = 1) AS lowest_percentage_increase;
"""
db.execute(sql)
```

```python
db.execute("""
```
```python
SELECT c.CustomerID,
       SUM(t.Price * t.Amount) AS TotalSpending,
       SUM(t.Price) / SUM(t.Amount) AS AvgPricePerSingleItem,
       c.Currency
FROM transactions_1k AS t
JOIN customers AS c
  ON t.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
GROUP BY c.CustomerID, c.Currency
ORDER BY TotalSpending DESC
LIMIT 1;
""")
```

```python
db.execute("""
SELECT 
  SUM(CASE WHEN p.Birthday = '1959-02-18' AND l.Date LIKE '1981-11-%' THEN l.`T-CHO` END) AS nov_sum,
  SUM(CASE WHEN p.Birthday = '1959-02-18' AND l.Date LIKE '1981-12-%' THEN l.`T-CHO` END) AS dec_sum,
  1.0 * (SUM(CASE WHEN p.Birthday = '1959-02-18' AND l.Date LIKE '1981-11-%' THEN l.`T-CHO` END)
       - SUM(CASE WHEN p.Birthday = '1959-02-18' AND l.Date LIKE '1981-12-%' THEN l.`T-CHO` END))
       / SUM(CASE WHEN p.Birthday = '1959-02-18' AND l.Date LIKE '1981-12-%' THEN l.`T-CHO` END) AS decrease_rate
FROM Laboratory AS l
JOIN Patient AS p ON l.ID = p.ID
WHERE p.Birthday = '1959-02-18'
  AND (l.Date LIKE '1981-11-%' OR l.Date LIKE '1981-12-%');
""")
```

  Q: Among the patients that died, what is the condition of the oldest patient?
  Hint: if deathdate is not null, it means this patient died; condition refers to DESCRIPTION from conditions; the oldest patient refers to MAX(SUBTRACT(strftime('%Y', deathdate), strftime('%Y', birthdate)));
  SQL: SELECT T1.DESCRIPTION FROM conditions AS T1 INNER JOIN patients AS T2 ON T1.PATIENT = T2.patient WHERE T2.deathdate IS NOT NULL ORDER BY strftime('%Y', T2.deathdate) - strftime('%Y', T2.birthdate) DESC LIMIT 1

FROM income
JOIN member ON income.link_to_member = member.member_id
WHERE income.date_received = '2019-09-09'

```python
  ON Y.CustomerID = C.CustomerID

LIMIT 1
""")
```

FINAL("WITH target_customer AS (SELECT CustomerID FROM transactions_1k WHERE Date = '2012-08-25' GROUP BY CustomerID HAVING ROUND(SUM(Amount * Price), 1) = 634.8), year_consumption AS (SELECT ym.CustomerID, SUM(CASE WHEN SUBSTR(ym.Date, 1, 4) = '2012' THEN ym.Consumption ELSE 0 END) AS consumption_2012, SUM(CASE WHEN SUBSTR(ym.Date, 1, 4) = '2013' THEN ym.Consumption ELSE 0 END) AS consumption_2013 FROM yearmonth AS ym JOIN target_customer AS tc ON ym.CustomerID = tc.CustomerID GROUP BY ym.CustomerID) SELECT 1.0 * (consumption_2012 - consumption_2013) / NULLIF(consumption_2012, 0) AS consumption_decrease_rate FROM year_consumption")

FINAL SQL: WITH target_customer AS (SELECT MIN(CustomerID) AS CustomerID FROM (SELECT CustomerID FROM transactions_1k WHERE Date = '2012-08-25' AND ROUND(Amount * Price, 1) = 634.8 UNION SELECT CustomerID FROM transactions_1k WHERE Date = '2012-08-25' GROUP BY CustomerID HAVING ROUND(SUM(Amount * Price), 1) = 634.8)) SELECT 1.0 * (SUM(CASE WHEN SUBSTR(Date, 1, 4) = '2012' THEN Consumption ELSE 0 END) - SUM(CASE WHEN SUBSTR(Date, 1, 4) = '2013' THEN Consumption ELSE 0 END)) / NULLIF(SUM(CASE WHEN SUBSTR(Date, 1, 4) = '2012' THEN Consumption ELSE 0 END), 0) AS consumption_decrease_rate FROM yearmonth WHERE CustomerID = (SELECT CustomerID FROM target_customer)
